beginState: s32'CmnActMatchWin'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnactmatchwin'
    playAnimation: s32'mll800cs', 0
    checkLastStateName: s32'WinActionWait'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      playCameraAnimation: s32'mll800cs', 23, 0, -1
    endIf: 
    else: 
      playCameraAnimation: s32'mll800cs', 23, 15, -1
    endElse: 
    cinesco: 1
    swapMeshSet: s32'MatchWin'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      resetSaturation: 1, 1
      setPostProcessSaturation: -1, 800, 50
      resetDiffusion: 1, 1
      setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 50
      setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 50
    endIf: 
    ifOnFrame: Val(5)
      characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_MLL_MatchWin'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
      resetDOF: 1, 1
      focalDistance: -1, 700, 0
      focalRegion: -1, 0, 0
      focalNearTransition: -1, 0, 0
      focalFarTransition: -1, 500, 0
      focalNearBlurSize: -1, 0, 0
      focalFarBlurSize: -1, 40, 30
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(70)
      postProcessEffect: s32'Overlay_win', 1, 40
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(90)
      createObject: s32'MLL_800CS_Twinkle', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    ifOnFrame: Val(178)
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx402demo'
      jimaku: s32'prev', -2147483618
      mouthPause: 0, 74
      demoEndOnMouthEnd: 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(80)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(8000)
        setPushboxWidthFront: 2, 45
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(0)

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_Dust_HomingJump'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(65000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(30000)
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(50)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            spriteBlend: s32'mll035_04', 2, 45
          endIf: 
          else: 
            spriteBlend: s32'mll035_05', 2, 45
            ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon:
